A fowl swallowed a diamond in a poultry and the owner of the diamond contracted a man to find the fowl and kill it. When the man arrived at the poultry, there were more than a thousand fowl in the poultry and only one was sitting by itself away from the others. He killed the one sitting by itself and that was the exact one that had swallowed the diamond. The amazed owner of the diamond asked: "How did you know it was that fowl?" He responded: "Very easy! When idiots get rich ...they dont mix with others." *LESSON* When God answers your long awaited prayers, maintain your normal profile. Dont be proud! Am far from ascertaining that dogs are better than humans,but I have observed something unique about dogs,that is very rare amongst humans.  If you pick up a starving dog and make him prosperous, he will never bite you. You can throw apples at an hungry man,after eating them can throw an arrow at you.       Dont contest this fact, you may have been a victim of betrayal. I have seen a mad dog afraid to bite it owner. I have seen children betrayed their parents,servants their masters, wives their husds. Even after making them prosperous from  starving conditions. ' . We as humans have existed for the sake of each other,so is either you teach them or learn to bear  with them.    Every time  things seem to go against you,dont loose your peace. The world is not here to give you peace,it is within you.... Accept whatever comes to you woven in the pattern of your destiny, for what could more aptly fit your needs?  The master playwright (God) has written the play for you the  actor or actress to perform. Farewells can be shattering, but returns are surely worse. Solid flesh can never live up to the bright shadow cast by its absence. Time and distance blur the edges; then suddenly the beloved has arrived, and its noon with its merciless light, and every spot and pore and wrinkle and bristle stands clear. ' . ADMISSION OPENS 2018-19 HEART SCHOOL OF AVIATION PONDICHERRY http://www.heartaviation.com/ ' .  *Wake Up Puducherry*  A call to all Ammas, Appas, Annas, Akkas to join the cause to raise our voice against Sexual Abuse *Let us come out of our slumber; let the collective consciousness of Puducherry challenge any forms of violence against girls and women in India.* Its shocking to know a gang raped the little girl Asifa, eight year old child. This is a chilly reminder to Indian mothers to express their voice. Another incident at Uttar Pradesh, a girl from Unnae was rape...d and the victims father was brutally assaulted and died. In a country where the female form, epitomize as a sacred divine creation, the nation is shamed when the attacks add to a grim catalogue of myriad sexual assaults all across India. The gory details of these assaults are getting more brutal and devastating day by day. These shameless and brutal cases shake the very foundation of our consciousness and our being. How can the collective consciousness of our society continue their daily chores without getting agitated and shamed? There may be groups which are protesting and condemning but what about a vast majority of our citizens. They continue their lives as if nothing has happened. This has to end; each one of us has the responsibility to come out of our slumber and take proactive steps to contribute to end violence against girls and women in our society. We, the *IRAIVAIS Team* from Puducherry urge INDIA to stand up against ASSAULT ON WOMEN, ASSAULT ON THE GIRL CHILD, and ASSAULT ON INDIAS FUTURE. LET US ALL COME TO EVOLVE A COLLECTIVE CONSCIOUSNESS AGAINST EXPLOITATION AND BARBARIC BEHAVIOUR AGAINST WOMEN AND GIRLS. THERE IS NO TIME FOR SILENCE, IT IS TIME FOR ACTION! *Puducherry IRAIVIS* See more ' . : See Translation ' .     ,   12.4.2018   ....See Translation ' .              ,     See Translation ' . Image: Watch Donald Trumps Victory Speech HERE (LIVE STREAM) - The ...' . LETS LEARN  FROM THIS!!!  Most Nigerians Currently feel like hanging Mr President. Particularly, the importers, due to the dollar rise. Ive been feeling the same way too, until until I had an encounter with a Chinese guy, and Ive tagged my feelings as stupidity.  This Chinese guy has a factory where he manufacture furniture here in Nigeria. One of his raw materials is wood, which he sources from Nigeria, because Nigerian wood is cheap and of the best quality. But he has to... import other accessories.  One of the amazing things is; since the rise of dollar, the guy has been importing accessories, yet he has not increased the price of his products, so how come?  This guy put his wife in charge of the factory, while he spends most of his time at Sagamu, in Ogun State, buying timber and exporting to China. The money from the exported timber that was supposed to be transfered back to him here in Nigeria, is been used to buy the furniture accessories he uses for production.  By so doing, he doesnt need to buy dollar. So he said "friend, I dont have problem with dollar rising to N500+ because I dont need it for anything" he said his Indian friend does the same thing with ginger export. While the only thing we Nigerians do is exporting our complaints on social media.  So the Indians and the Chinese are busy coming up with strategies that have defied the dollar challenge, while we Nigerians are shouting "dollar is high."  Again, it is all about taking advantage of the situation to move ahead instead of just wailing on social media.  Lets all start THINKING about DOING even as we criticise government policies we dont like!#Copied See more ' . POLITICS:  Lessons From The Mosquito                      ============= A young mosquito went out flying for the first time in its life. The father asked "How does it feel?" The mosquito replied, "it was GREAT! Everyone was clapping for me." The father replied,  "They werent clapping for you, they wanted to kill you, the more they clapped, the more chances you are likely to die. E ADAB SE PESH AANA OR KAHNA KI ALLAH NE APKO YAAD KIYA HAI OR ALLAH NE APKO USKE DEEDAR KE LIYE BULAYA HAI JAB JIBRAEEL AMIN AAP MUSA (A.S) KE  PAAS AAYE OR FARMAYA KI YA MUSA (A.S) APKO ALLAH NE YAAD KIYA HAI TO APNE FARMAYA KYU ? TO JIBRAEEL AMIN NE KAH DIYA KI MEIN APKI ROOH KABZ KARNE AAYA HU  OR ALLAH KA HUKUM HAI ITNA KAHNA THA KI AAP MUSA (A.S ) NE EK THAPPAD RASID KAR DIYA  APKE EK THAPPAD SE HAZRATE JIBRAEEL KI AANKH NIKAL BAHAR AA GAI... ALLAH NE FARMAYA HAI KI  AAP TO KABSE ALLAH KA DEEDAR KARNA CHAHTE THE OR AAJ INKAAR KAR RAHE HO  JAB KI APKO KHUD ALLAH NE APNE DEEDAR KO BULAYA HAI FIR KYA THA..JIBRAEEL A.S WAPAS AAYE  OR JAISA ALLAH NE FARMAYA  APNE MUSA A.S KO KAH DIYA JAB MUSA A.S NE YE SUNA TO KAHA KI AE JIBRAEEL SUNO MUJHE THODI MOHALAT DO.. TO AAP JIBRAEEL WAPAS ALLAH KE PAAS AAYE OR SAARA HAAL BAYAN KAR DIYA EK BAAT YAAD RAHE KI ALLAH NE MUSA A.S KO 9 MOZIZA ATA KIYE THE JAB  FIRON OR USKI SAINA AAP MUSA A.S KO KHATM KARNE KE LIYE .. Assalamo Alaykum Aap jante hai ..jab Hazrat musa (a.s) ko Allah ne Nabuwat di to Allah ne farmaya ki Ae musa..firon zamin pe fasad fela raha hai or kahna ki Allah ke siwa koi mabood nahi  Jab musa (a.s) firon ki or gaye to musa a.s ne farmaya ki  Ae firon mein Allah ka paigambar hu Or Allah par imaan le Aa... To firon ne kaha mein hi khuda hu Or meri hi hukumat hai Or agar tu paigambar hai to musa tu hame kuch Aisa dikha ..ki sach me khuda hai  Ek baat yaad rahe musa a.s ko Allah ne 9 mojiza Ata farmaya Par firon nahi mana or kaha ki agar tu saccha hai to kuch kar ke dikha  Hum kal dekhenge ki tu kitna saccha hai . Jab musa ne kaha ki thik hai kal tu jiske bhi samne mujhe khada karega par mein gaalib rahunga Idhar firon ne kitne jaadugaro ko alag alag mulk se bulaya  e e jadugar aaye Jab firon ne kaha pahle kon dikhayega To musa a.s ne kaha ki mein dikhata hu  To jab musa a.s ne apni chadi zamin pe dali to wo kuch aisa mojiza hua ki sabhi jaadugar sazde me pad gaye  Fir bhi firon nahi mana or kaha ki tu to khula jaadugar hai Or jo dusre jadugar the wo imaan le aaye par firon nahi laaya Aakhir me jab firon ne musa a.s ko marne ke liye apne sipaahiyo ko sath lekar uss Samundar ki or gaye to Musa a.s ko Allah ne farmaya ki Ae musa apni chadi ko iss pani par maaro To jaise hi apne chadi mari to pani ke bich rasta  gaya or musa a.s andar aaye or jab firon ki saina aayi or firon sabko paani me dubo diya.. Mere dosto meine ye kissa isliye share kiya ki jo Allah ka ho jata hai Allah uska ho jata hai See more ' . Notes that African migrants from nations including Nigeria, Guinea, Senegal, Mali, Niger and Gambia make the dangerous crossing through the Sahara to Libya with hopes of making it over the Mediterranean Sea to Italy and other European countries in search of greener pastures; Also notes that on November 14, 2017, the US Television Network, CNN broke the news of auctioning of human beings in Libya with a live footage of the auction in which young men were sold to North African buyers as potential farmhands; and one of the unidentified young men sold off for as little as $400 (N144,000) in the grainy cell phone video obtained by CNN is a Nigerian in his twenties; Further notes that the footage of the auctioning of Black Africans in the conflict-torn nation sparked outrage across the world with thousands of people taking to the streets of Paris, France to protest against the modern day slavery, and in reaction, the African Union, on November 17,2017 called on the Libyan Authorities to investogate the matter; Resolves to: (i) Urge the Federal Government to liase with the Government of Libya to find a solution to the menace of migration and modern day slavery in Libya; and (ii) Mandate Committees on Human Rights and Foreign Affairs to interface with the Ministry of foreign affairs and relevant stakeholders to identify the factors that encourage the migrantsnto embark on the perilous journey, proffer solutions that would discourage same and then provide for how the Nigerian Youths caught in the web would return to the country and report back to the House within four (4) weeks for further legislative action. The news which was reported exclusively by Secrets Reporters is currently causing uproar in the Presidency. Information made available to this newspaper is that top presidential aides of Northern extraction led by the National Security Adviser, Dasuki have been mandated to reach out to the Emirs of the regions sympathetic to the President to beg the PDP boss to withdraw his resignation letter. Freshers 2k17 ' . Nafrat Nahi Adhikar Chahiye Siksha Aur Rozgar Chahiye !  Student-Youth Yatra to start on 7th November from Chandigarh....  The Yatra will go through the states of Delhi, UP, Bihar, Jharkhand and culminate in Kolkata on the 21st November. The Narendra Modi government has completed three years term in power. What has unfolded for the student youth in last three years is a regime of push out from opportunities of education and employment. A government that came to power promising 1 crore new jobs every year has in reality delivered lowest job growth in last eight years. If in formal sector number of jobs reduced by 70 lakh in 2016 alone, demonetisation has caused havoc in the employment scenario of informal sector. The reality of much touted Make in India is such that massive lay off is happening in white collar jobs in IT sector as well. A policy of fund-cut, seat-cut, NET-cut, fellowship-cut and fee-hike is being imposed in education. While the education budget got reduced to 3.65% of the total budget in 2016-17 as compared to an already minuscule share of 4.57% in 2013-14, tax exemption too corporates reached a record high of 83,492 crores in 2016-17 itself. We are seeing our ks starving as loan amounting to 13 lakh crores given to big corporates have been declared as unrecovered "" loans. And these are same time when Junaid, Pehlu, Akhlaq, Zafar are being killed. When accused in Pehlus murder are being acquitted and state backed lawyer is supporting the accused in Junaids case. Communally motivated debates over taj mahal and gau raksha are being thrown at us. At such a juncture AISA-RYA appeals student-youth of the country to join the Yatra and demand -  *Stop job cuts, fulfil the promise of 1 crore new jobs per year! *Fill vacancies in all government jobs without delay! *End contractualization, guarantee secure and dignified employment! *End the regime of fee hike, seat cut, NET cut, fund cut in education! *End corporate loot, increase budgetary expenditure for education and employment! *Ensure womens freedom, equality, and safety! Establish GSCASH in all institutions! *End communal-casteist mob violence! #AISA See more ' . WISH YOU ALL A VERY HAPPY DIWALI ' . Happy birthday ' . ............... ........!   , ,    [English translation is given below]          ...                  ,                   ,     ,                       , , ,              ,                                ,                       ,         ? --- () Shiva (Lord Shiva) + ratri (night), so Shivaratri means the night of Lord Shiva. Every lunar month on the 13th or 14th day of the dark half of the moon phase there is a Shivaratri but in the Vedic month of Phalgun (February-March ) there is a Maha Shivaratri. The ceremony takes place mainly at night, which is observed in the honour of Lord Shiva, who was married to Parvati (Mother Durga) on this day. Devotees of Lord Shiva generally observe a strict fast on this day and some go to the extent of a nirjal fast i.e. they do not even have a sip of water. They stay awake the entire night. The Shiva lingam is worshipped throughout the night by washing it every three hours with milk, yogurt, ghee, honey and so forth, whilst chanting of the mantra Om namah shivaya, continues. Offering of bael leaves are made to the Lingam. Bael leaves are very sacred (as Tulsi to Lord Vishnu and dhar to Mother Durga ar See moreSee Translation ' .
